# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
7 strategies to scale your database

1)Indexing
- Check the qurey pattern of your application and create the right indexes


2) Materialized Views 

Pre-compute complex query results and store them for faster access

3) Denormalization
Reduce complex joins to improve query performance


4)Vertical Scaling
Boost your database server by adding more  CPU, RAM and storage 


5)Caching
Store frequently accessed data in a faster storage layer to reduce database load

6)Replication
Create replicas of your primary database on different servers for scaling the reads


7)Sharding
Split your database tables into smaller pieces and spread them across servers.
Used for scaling the writes as well as the threads

















 ^toyY6EEK
